- **>8% conversi√≥n** de asistentes a compradores

### **Caracter√≠sticas √önicas**

- **Framework Replicable**: Escalable a cualquier nicho o audiencia

```javascript
  registrations: 0,
  attendees: 0,
  conversions: 0,
  revenue: 0,
  
  update: function(type, value) {
    this[type] += value;
    this.updateDisplay();
  },

    document.getElementById('registrations').textContent = this.registrations;
    document.getElementById('attendees').textContent = this.attendees;
    document.getElementById('conversions').textContent = this.conversions;
```

## ü§ñ SISTEMA DE AUTOMATIZACI√ìN AVANZADA

### **Automatizaci√≥n de Contenido Din√°mico**

#### **Segmentaci√≥n de Audiencia en Tiempo Real**
```javascript
const audienceSegmentation = {
  segments: {
    beginner: {
      criteria: ["nunca_ia", "basica_ia"],
      slides: ["hook_basico", "demo_simple", "oferta_basica"],
      script: "script_principiante"
    },
    intermediate: {
      criteria: ["intermedia_ia", "usa_chatgpt"],
      slides: ["hook_avanzado", "demo_complejo", "oferta_premium"],
      script: "script_intermedio"
    },
    advanced: {
      criteria: ["avanzada_ia", "desarrollador"],
      slides: ["hook_tecnico", "demo_api", "oferta_enterprise"],
      script: "script_avanzado"
    }
  },
  
  detectSegment: function(responses) {
    // Analizar respuestas de encuestas para determinar segmento
    if (responses.experience === "nunca" || responses.experience === "basica") {
      return this.segments.beginner;
    } else if (responses.experience === "intermedia") {
      return this.segments.intermediate;
    } else {
      return this.segments.advanced;
    }
  },
  
  adaptContent: function(segment) {
    // Cambiar slides y script seg√∫n segmento detectado
    this.loadSlides(segment.slides);
    this.loadScript(segment.script);
  }
};
```

#### **Personalizaci√≥n de Ofertas**
```javascript
const offerPersonalization = {
  baseOffer: {
    price: 497,
    bonuses: ["prompts", "plantillas", "comunidad"]
  },
  
  personalizedOffers: {
    beginner: {
      price: 297,
      bonuses: ["prompts", "plantillas", "comunidad", "curso_basico"],
      payment_plans: ["pago_unico", "3_cuotas"]
    },
    intermediate: {
      price: 497,
      bonuses: ["prompts", "plantillas", "comunidad", "herramientas_avanzadas"],
      payment_plans: ["pago_unico", "6_cuotas"]
    },
    advanced: {
      price: 997,
      bonuses: ["prompts", "plantillas", "comunidad", "herramientas_avanzadas", "api_access", "soporte_prioritario"],
      payment_plans: ["pago_unico", "12_cuotas"]
    }
  },
  
  generateOffer: function(segment, engagement_score) {
    const baseOffer = this.personalizedOffers[segment];
    
    // Ajustar precio seg√∫n engagement
    if (engagement_score > 80) {
      baseOffer.price *= 0.8; // 20% descuento por alto engagement
    }
    
    return baseOffer;
  }
};
```

### **Sistema de A/B Testing Automatizado**

#### **Testing de Variantes en Tiempo Real**
```javascript
const abTesting = {
  variants: {
    hook: ["shock_emocional", "revelacion_prohibida", "pregunta_existencial"],
    credibility: ["credenciales_tecnicas", "resultados_comprobables", "historia_personal"],
    offer: ["precio_lanzamiento", "bonos_masivos", "acceso_vip"],
    cta: ["accion_inmediata", "urgencia", "escasez"]
  },
  
  currentTests: {},
  
  startTest: function(testName, variants) {
    this.currentTests[testName] = {
      variants: variants,
      results: {},
      startTime: new Date()
    };
  },
  
  selectVariant: function(testName) {
    const test = this.currentTests[testName];
    if (!test) return null;
    
    // Seleccionar variante basada en performance actual
    const bestVariant = this.getBestPerformingVariant(testName);
    return bestVariant || test.variants[0];
  },
  
  trackResult: function(testName, variant, result) {
    if (!this.currentTests[testName].results[variant]) {
      this.currentTests[testName].results[variant] = {
        impressions: 0,
        conversions: 0,
        revenue: 0
      };
    }
    
    this.currentTests[testName].results[variant].impressions++;
    if (result.converted) {
      this.currentTests[testName].results[variant].conversions++;
      this.currentTests[testName].results[variant].revenue += result.value;
    }
  }
};
```

---

## üìä SISTEMA DE ANALYTICS PREDICTIVO

### **Predicci√≥n de Conversi√≥n en Tiempo Real**

#### **Modelo de Machine Learning**
```javascript
const predictiveAnalytics = {
  model: {
    features: [
      'time_on_slide',
      'engagement_score',
      'survey_responses',
      'chat_activity',
      'previous_behavior'
    ],
    
    weights: {
      'time_on_slide': 0.25,
      'engagement_score': 0.30,
      'survey_responses': 0.20,
      'chat_activity': 0.15,
      'previous_behavior': 0.10
    }
  },
  
  calculateConversionProbability: function(userData) {
    let score = 0;
    
    // Calcular score basado en features
    for (const feature of this.model.features) {
      if (userData[feature]) {
        score += userData[feature] * this.model.weights[feature];
      }
    }
    
    // Convertir score a probabilidad (0-100%)
    return Math.min(100, Math.max(0, score * 100));
  },
  
  getRecommendations: function(probability) {
    if (probability > 80) {
      return {
        action: "push_offer",
        urgency: "high",
        discount: 0
      };
    } else if (probability > 60) {
      return {
        action: "increase_urgency",
        urgency: "medium",
        discount: 0.1
      };
    } else {
      return {
        action: "build_trust",
        urgency: "low",
        discount: 0.2
      };
    }
  }
};
```

#### **Dashboard de Predicciones**
```javascript
const predictionDashboard = {
  users: {},
  
  updateUser: function(userId, data) {
    if (!this.users[userId]) {
      this.users[userId] = {
        id: userId,
        joinTime: new Date(),
        data: {}
      };
    }
    
    this.users[userId].data = { ...this.users[userId].data, ...data };
    this.users[userId].conversionProbability = predictiveAnalytics.calculateConversionProbability(this.users[userId].data);
    this.users[userId].recommendations = predictiveAnalytics.getRecommendations(this.users[userId].conversionProbability);
  },
  
  getHighProbabilityUsers: function() {
    return Object.values(this.users)
      .filter(user => user.conversionProbability > 70)
      .sort((a, b) => b.conversionProbability - a.conversionProbability);
  },
  
  getLowEngagementUsers: function() {
    return Object.values(this.users)
      .filter(user => user.conversionProbability < 30)
      .sort((a, b) => a.conversionProbability - b.conversionProbability);
  }
};
```

---

## üéØ SISTEMA DE SEGMENTACI√ìN AVANZADA

### **Perfiles de Audiencia Din√°micos**

#### **Segmentaci√≥n por Comportamiento**
```javascript
const behaviorSegmentation = {
  profiles: {
    "early_adopter": {
      characteristics: ["high_engagement", "quick_decision", "tech_savvy"],
      slides: ["hook_innovacion", "demo_avanzado", "oferta_premium"],
      timing: "fast_pace",
      cta: "exclusividad"
    },
    
    "analytical": {
      characteristics: ["high_engagement", "slow_decision", "data_driven"],
      slides: ["hook_estadisticas", "demo_detallado", "oferta_con_garantia"],
      timing: "slow_pace",
      cta: "garantia"
    },
    
    "skeptical": {
      characteristics: ["low_engagement", "high_questions", "risk_averse"],
      slides: ["hook_testimonios", "demo_simple", "oferta_con_prueba"],
      timing: "very_slow",
      cta: "sin_riesgo"
    },
    
    "price_sensitive": {
      characteristics: ["medium_engagement", "price_focused", "comparison_shopper"],
      slides: ["hook_ahorro", "demo_valor", "oferta_descuento"],
      timing: "medium_pace",
      cta: "descuento"
    }
  },
  
  detectProfile: function(userBehavior) {
    let bestMatch = null;
    let bestScore = 0;
    
    for (const [profileName, profile] of Object.entries(this.profiles)) {
      let score = 0;
      
      for (const characteristic of profile.characteristics) {
        if (userBehavior[characteristic]) {
          score += 1;
        }
      }
      
      if (score > bestScore) {
        bestScore = score;
        bestMatch = profileName;
      }
    }
    
    return bestMatch;
  }
};
```

#### **Personalizaci√≥n de Timing**
```javascript
const timingOptimization = {
  defaultTiming: {
    hook: 30,
    credibility: 120,
    problem: 180,
    solution: 300,
    demo: 600,
    offer: 900,
    cta: 1200
  },
  
  adaptiveTiming: {
    fast_pace: {
      hook: 20,
      credibility: 90,
      problem: 120,
      solution: 240,
      demo: 480,
      offer: 720,
      cta: 900
    },
    
    slow_pace: {
      hook: 45,
      credibility: 180,
      problem: 270,
      solution: 450,
      demo: 900,
      offer: 1350,
      cta: 1800
    }
  },
  
  adjustTiming: function(profile, engagement) {
    const baseTiming = this.adaptiveTiming[profile.timing] || this.defaultTiming;
    
    // Ajustar seg√∫n engagement
    const multiplier = engagement > 80 ? 0.8 : engagement < 40 ? 1.3 : 1.0;
    
    const adjustedTiming = {};
    for (const [phase, time] of Object.entries(baseTiming)) {
      adjustedTiming[phase] = Math.round(time * multiplier);
    }
    
    return adjustedTiming;
  }
};
```

---

## üîÑ SISTEMA DE OPTIMIZACI√ìN CONTINUA

### **Auto-Optimizaci√≥n Basada en Datos**

#### **Optimizaci√≥n Autom√°tica de Conversi√≥n**
```javascript
const autoOptimization = {
  metrics: {
    conversion_rate: 0,
    engagement_rate: 0,
    revenue_per_attendee: 0,
    time_to_conversion: 0
  },
  
  thresholds: {
    min_conversion_rate: 0.05,
    min_engagement_rate: 0.60,
    min_revenue_per_attendee: 400
  },
  
  optimize: function(currentMetrics) {
    const optimizations = [];
    
    if (currentMetrics.conversion_rate < this.thresholds.min_conversion_rate) {
      optimizations.push({
        type: "increase_urgency",
        action: "reduce_price",
        value: 0.1
      });
      
      optimizations.push({
        type: "improve_offer",
        action: "add_bonus",
        value: "soporte_extra"
      });
    }
    
    if (currentMetrics.engagement_rate < this.thresholds.min_engagement_rate) {
      optimizations.push({
        type: "increase_engagement",
        action: "add_interaction",
        value: "encuesta_extra"
      });
    }
    
    if (currentMetrics.revenue_per_attendee < this.thresholds.min_revenue_per_attendee) {
      optimizations.push({
        type: "increase_value",
        action: "upsell",
        value: "version_premium"
      });
    }
    
    return optimizations;
  },
  
  applyOptimizations: function(optimizations) {
    for (const optimization of optimizations) {
      this.executeOptimization(optimization);
    }
  }
};
```

#### **Sistema de Alertas Inteligentes**
```javascript
const intelligentAlerts = {
  alerts: [],
  
  checkMetrics: function(metrics) {
    this.alerts = [];
    
    // Alerta de baja conversi√≥n
    if (metrics.conversion_rate < 0.03) {
      this.alerts.push({
        type: "critical",
        message: "Conversi√≥n muy baja: " + (metrics.conversion_rate * 100).toFixed(1) + "%",
        action: "reducir_precio_20%",
        priority: "high"
      });
    }
    
    // Alerta de alto abandono
    if (metrics.abandonment_rate > 0.40) {
      this.alerts.push({
        type: "warning",
        message: "Alto abandono: " + (metrics.abandonment_rate * 100).toFixed(1) + "%",
        action: "aumentar_engagement",
        priority: "medium"
      });
    }
    
    // Alerta de bajo engagement
    if (metrics.engagement_rate < 0.50) {
      this.alerts.push({
        type: "warning",
        message: "Bajo engagement: " + (metrics.engagement_rate * 100).toFixed(1) + "%",
        action: "agregar_interacciones",
        priority: "medium"
      });
    }
    
    return this.alerts;
  },
  
  sendAlert: function(alert) {
    // Enviar alerta al presentador
    console.log(`üö® ALERTA ${alert.type.toUpperCase()}: ${alert.message}`);
    console.log(`üìã ACCI√ìN RECOMENDADA: ${alert.action}`);
    
    // Enviar notificaci√≥n push si es cr√≠tica
    if (alert.priority === "high") {
      this.sendPushNotification(alert);
    }
  }
};
```

### **Notificaciones en Tiempo Real**

#### **Sistema de Notificaciones Push**
```javascript
const notificationSystem = {
  notifications: [],
  
  sendNotification: function(type, message, data) {
    const notification = {
      id: Date.now(),
      type: type,
      message: message,
      data: data,
      timestamp: new Date(),
      read: false
    };
    
    this.notifications.push(notification);
    this.displayNotification(notification);
    
    // Enviar a dispositivos m√≥viles si est√° configurado
    if (this.isMobileEnabled()) {
      this.sendMobileNotification(notification);
    }
  },
  
  displayNotification: function(notification) {
    const notificationElement = document.createElement('div');
    notificationElement.className = `notification notification-${notification.type}`;
    notificationElement.innerHTML = `
      <div class="notification-content">
        <h4>${this.getNotificationTitle(notification.type)}</h4>
        <p>${notification.message}</p>
        <button onclick="this.parentElement.parentElement.remove()">Cerrar</button>
      </div>
    `;
    
    document.body.appendChild(notificationElement);
    
    // Auto-remove despu√©s de 10 segundos
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (notificationElement.parentElement) {
        notificationElement.remove();
      }
    }, 10000);
  },
  
  getNotificationTitle: function(type) {
    const titles = {
      'conversion': 'üéâ Nueva Conversi√≥n!',
      'alert': '‚ö†Ô∏è Alerta del Sistema',
      'optimization': 'üîß Optimizaci√≥n Aplicada',
      'engagement': 'üìà Engagement Alto',
      'abandonment': 'üìâ Abandono Detectado'
    };
    
    return titles[type] || 'üì¢ Notificaci√≥n';
  }
};
```

```javascript
const dynamicThemes = {
  themes: {
    professional: {
      colors: {
        primary: "#1E3A8A",
        secondary: "#059669",
        accent: "#DC2626",
        background: "#F8FAFC"
      },
      fonts: {
        title: "Inter Bold",
        body: "Inter Regular"
      },
      style: "clean_minimal"
    },
    
    energetic: {
      colors: {
        primary: "#FF6B35",
        secondary: "#F7931E",
        accent: "#FFD23F",
        background: "#2C3E50"
      },
      fonts: {
        title: "Montserrat Bold",
        body: "Open Sans"
      },
      style: "bold_vibrant"
    },
    
    tech: {
      colors: {
        primary: "#00D4FF",
        secondary: "#0099CC",
        accent: "#FF3366",
        background: "#0A0A0A"
      },
      fonts: {
        title: "Roboto Mono Bold",
        body: "Roboto"
      },
      style: "futuristic"
    }
  },
  
  selectTheme: function(audienceProfile) {
    switch (audienceProfile) {
      case "early_adopter":
        return this.themes.tech;
      case "analytical":
        return this.themes.professional;
      case "skeptical":
        return this.themes.professional;
      case "price_sensitive":
        return this.themes.energetic;
      default:
        return this.themes.professional;
    }
  },
  
  applyTheme: function(theme) {
    const root = document.documentElement;
    
    // Aplicar colores
    root.style.setProperty('--primary-color', theme.colors.primary);
    root.style.setProperty('--secondary-color', theme.colors.secondary);
    root.style.setProperty('--accent-color', theme.colors.accent);
    root.style.setProperty('--background-color', theme.colors.background);
    
    // Aplicar fuentes
    root.style.setProperty('--title-font', theme.fonts.title);
    root.style.setProperty('--body-font', theme.fonts.body);
    
    // Aplicar estilo
    document.body.className = `theme-${theme.style}`;
  }
};
```

```javascript
const executiveDashboard = {
  generateReport: function() {
    const report = {
      timestamp: new Date(),
      summary: this.getSummary(),
      metrics: this.getMetrics(),
      insights: this.getInsights(),
      recommendations: this.getRecommendations()
    };
    
    return report;
  },
  
  getSummary: function() {
    return {
      total_attendees: metrics.attendees,
      conversion_rate: (metrics.conversions / metrics.attendees * 100).toFixed(1) + "%",
      revenue_generated: "$" + metrics.revenue.toLocaleString(),
      roi: ((metrics.revenue / 50000) * 100).toFixed(1) + "%"
    };
  },
  
  getInsights: function() {
    const insights = [];
    
    if (metrics.conversion_rate > 0.08) {
      insights.push("üéØ Conversi√≥n excelente - superando objetivo del 8%");
    }
    
    if (metrics.engagement_rate > 0.80) {
      insights.push("üìà Engagement alto - audiencia muy comprometida");
    }
    
    if (metrics.abandonment_rate < 0.20) {
      insights.push("‚úÖ Bajo abandono - contenido muy relevante");
    }
    
    return insights;
  },
  
  getRecommendations: function() {
    const recommendations = [];
    
    if (metrics.conversion_rate < 0.05) {
      recommendations.push("Considerar reducir precio en 20%");
    }
    
    if (metrics.engagement_rate < 0.60) {
      recommendations.push("Agregar m√°s interacciones y encuestas");
    }
    
    if (metrics.time_to_conversion > 1200) {
      recommendations.push("Acelerar el timing de la oferta");
    }
    
    return recommendations;
  }
};
```

## üß† SISTEMA DE INTELIGENCIA ARTIFICIAL AVANZADA

### **IA Predictiva para Conversi√≥n M√°xima**

#### **Modelo de Machine Learning Avanzado**
```python
import tensorflow as tf
import numpy as np
from sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestClassifier
from sklearn.neural_network import MLPClassifier

class WebinarConversionAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.model = self.build_neural_network()
        self.feature_importance = {}
        self.conversion_threshold = 0.75
        
    def build_neural_network(self):
        """Construir red neuronal para predicci√≥n de conversi√≥n"""
        model = tf.keras.Sequential([
            tf.keras.layers.Dense(128, activation='relu', input_shape=(50,)),
            tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.3),
            tf.keras.layers.Dense(64, activation='relu'),
            tf.keras.layers.Dropout(0.2),
            tf.keras.layers.Dense(32, activation='relu'),
            tf.keras.layers.Dense(1, activation='sigmoid')
        ])
        
        model.compile(
            optimizer='adam',
            loss='binary_crossentropy',
            metrics=['accuracy', 'precision', 'recall']
        )
        
        return model
    
    def extract_features(self, user_data):
        """Extraer 50 features clave del comportamiento del usuario"""
        features = np.array([
            user_data['time_on_hook'],
            user_data['engagement_score'],
            user_data['survey_responses'],
            user_data['chat_activity'],
            user_data['click_behavior'],
            user_data['scroll_depth'],
            user_data['device_type'],
            user_data['location'],
            user_data['previous_webinars'],
            user_data['email_engagement'],
            user_data['social_media_activity'],
            user_data['purchase_history'],
            user_data['demographic_score'],
            user_data['psychographic_score'],
            user_data['behavioral_score'],
            user_data['temporal_factors'],
            user_data['content_preferences'],
            user_data['interaction_patterns'],
            user_data['attention_span'],
            user_data['decision_speed'],
            user_data['risk_tolerance'],
            user_data['price_sensitivity'],
            user_data['social_proof_response'],
            user_data['authority_response'],
            user_data['scarcity_response'],
            user_data['urgency_response'],
            user_data['reciprocity_response'],
            user_data['commitment_response'],
            user_data['consistency_response'],
            user_data['liking_response'],
            user_data['consensus_response'],
            user_data['novelty_seeking'],
            user_data['tech_savviness'],
            user_data['learning_style'],
            user_data['communication_preference'],
            user_data['motivation_type'],
            user_data['goal_alignment'],
            user_data['pain_point_intensity'],
            user_data['solution_fit'],
            user_data['trust_level'],
            user_data['credibility_perception'],
            user_data['value_perception'],
            user_data['competitor_awareness'],
            user_data['budget_availability'],
            user_data['decision_authority'],
            user_data['timeline_urgency'],
            user_data['implementation_readiness'],
            user_data['support_needs'],
            user_data['success_probability'],
            user_data['retention_likelihood']
        ])
        
        return features.reshape(1, -1)
    
    def predict_conversion(self, user_data):
        """Predecir probabilidad de conversi√≥n"""
        features = self.extract_features(user_data)
        probability = self.model.predict(features)[0][0]
        
        return {
            'conversion_probability': probability,
            'confidence_level': self.calculate_confidence(probability),
            'recommended_action': self.get_recommended_action(probability),
            'optimal_timing': self.get_optimal_timing(probability),
            'personalized_offer': self.generate_personalized_offer(user_data, probability)
        }
    
    def calculate_confidence(self, probability):
        """Calcular nivel de confianza de la predicci√≥n"""
        if probability > 0.8 or probability < 0.2:
            return 'high'
        elif probability > 0.6 or probability < 0.4:
            return 'medium'
        else:
            return 'low'
    
    def get_recommended_action(self, probability):
        """Obtener acci√≥n recomendada basada en probabilidad"""
        if probability > 0.8:
            return {
                'action': 'immediate_offer',
                'urgency': 'high',
                'discount': 0,
                'bonus': 'premium_support'
            }
        elif probability > 0.6:
            return {
                'action': 'build_urgency',
                'urgency': 'medium',
                'discount': 0.1,
                'bonus': 'extra_bonus'
            }
        elif probability > 0.4:
            return {
                'action': 'increase_trust',
                'urgency': 'low',
                'discount': 0.2,
                'bonus': 'guarantee'
            }
        else:
            return {
                'action': 'nurture_relationship',
                'urgency': 'none',
                'discount': 0.3,
                'bonus': 'free_trial'
            }
    
    def get_optimal_timing(self, probability):
        """Determinar timing √≥ptimo para la oferta"""
        if probability > 0.8:
            return 'immediate'
        elif probability > 0.6:
            return 'within_5_minutes'
        elif probability > 0.4:
            return 'within_15_minutes'
        else:
            return 'follow_up_sequence'
    
    def generate_personalized_offer(self, user_data, probability):
        """Generar oferta personalizada basada en perfil del usuario"""
        base_price = 497
        
        # Ajustar precio seg√∫n probabilidad de conversi√≥n
        if probability > 0.8:
            price = base_price
            bonuses = ['premium_support', 'api_access', 'priority_implementation']
        elif probability > 0.6:
            price = base_price * 0.9
            bonuses = ['extra_bonus', 'extended_support']
        elif probability > 0.4:
            price = base_price * 0.8
            bonuses = ['guarantee', 'free_trial']
        else:
            price = base_price * 0.7
            bonuses = ['free_trial', 'money_back_guarantee']
        
        return {
            'price': price,
            'bonuses': bonuses,
            'payment_plans': self.get_payment_plans(probability),
            'urgency_level': self.get_urgency_level(probability),
            'scarcity_elements': self.get_scarcity_elements(probability)
        }
```

#### **Sistema de An√°lisis de Sentimientos en Tiempo Real**
```python
import nltk
from textblob import TextBlob
from vaderSentiment.vaderSentiment import SentimentIntensityAnalyzer

class SentimentAnalysisAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.analyzer = SentimentIntensityAnalyzer()
        self.sentiment_thresholds = {
            'positive': 0.1,
            'neutral': -0.1,
            'negative': -0.1
        }
    
    def analyze_chat_sentiment(self, chat_messages):
        """Analizar sentimiento de mensajes de chat en tiempo real"""
        sentiments = []
        
        for message in chat_messages:
            sentiment = self.analyzer.polarity_scores(message['text'])
            sentiments.append({
                'message': message['text'],
                'sentiment': sentiment,
                'timestamp': message['timestamp'],
                'user_id': message['user_id']
            })
        
        return self.aggregate_sentiment(sentiments)
    
    def aggregate_sentiment(self, sentiments):
        """Agregar sentimientos para obtener tendencia general"""
        if not sentiments:
            return {'overall': 'neutral', 'score': 0, 'confidence': 0}
        
        avg_compound = sum(s['sentiment']['compound'] for s in sentiments) / len(sentiments)
        
        if avg_compound > self.sentiment_thresholds['positive']:
            overall = 'positive'
        elif avg_compound < self.sentiment_thresholds['negative']:
            overall = 'negative'
        else:
            overall = 'neutral'
        
        return {
            'overall': overall,
            'score': avg_compound,
            'confidence': abs(avg_compound),
            'trend': self.calculate_trend(sentiments),
            'recommendations': self.get_sentiment_recommendations(overall, avg_compound)
        }
    
    def calculate_trend(self, sentiments):
        """Calcular tendencia del sentimiento a lo largo del tiempo"""
        if len(sentiments) < 2:
            return 'stable'
        
        # Dividir en dos mitades y comparar
        mid_point = len(sentiments) // 2
        first_half = sentiments[:mid_point]
        second_half = sentiments[mid_point:]
        
        first_avg = sum(s['sentiment']['compound'] for s in first_half) / len(first_half)
        second_avg = sum(s['sentiment']['compound'] for s in second_half) / len(second_half)
        
        if second_avg > first_avg + 0.1:
            return 'improving'
        elif second_avg < first_avg - 0.1:
            return 'declining'
        else:
            return 'stable'
    
    def get_sentiment_recommendations(self, overall, score):
        """Obtener recomendaciones basadas en sentimiento"""
        recommendations = []
        
        if overall == 'negative' and score < -0.3:
            recommendations.extend([
                'increase_engagement',
                'address_concerns',
                'provide_more_value',
                'reduce_price_pressure'
            ])
        elif overall == 'positive' and score > 0.3:
            recommendations.extend([
                'capitalize_on_momentum',
                'increase_urgency',
                'present_offer',
                'leverage_social_proof'
            ])
        else:
            recommendations.extend([
                'maintain_engagement',
                'build_trust',
                'provide_education',
                'gather_feedback'
            ])
        
        return recommendations
```

---

## üéØ SISTEMA DE OPTIMIZACI√ìN AUTOM√ÅTICA

### **Auto-Optimizaci√≥n Basada en IA**

#### **Algoritmo de Optimizaci√≥n Continua**
```python
import optuna
from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, precision_score, recall_score

class WebinarOptimizationAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.study = optuna.create_study(direction='maximize')
        self.optimization_history = []
        self.current_best_params = {}
    
    def optimize_webinar_parameters(self, historical_data):
        """Optimizar par√°metros del webinar usando Optuna"""
        
        def objective(trial):
            # Par√°metros a optimizar
            hook_duration = trial.suggest_int('hook_duration', 20, 60)
            credibility_duration = trial.suggest_int('credibility_duration', 90, 180)
            problem_duration = trial.suggest_int('problem_duration', 120, 240)
            solution_duration = trial.suggest_int('solution_duration', 180, 360)
            demo_duration = trial.suggest_int('demo_duration', 300, 600)
            offer_duration = trial.suggest_int('offer_duration', 180, 360)
            cta_duration = trial.suggest_int('cta_duration', 60, 120)
            
            # Par√°metros de contenido
            hook_type = trial.suggest_categorical('hook_type', 
                ['shock_emocional', 'revelacion_prohibida', 'pregunta_existencial'])
            credibility_type = trial.suggest_categorical('credibility_type',
                ['credenciales_tecnicas', 'resultados_comprobables', 'historia_personal'])
            offer_type = trial.suggest_categorical('offer_type',
                ['precio_lanzamiento', 'bonos_masivos', 'acceso_vip'])
            
            # Par√°metros de precio
            base_price = trial.suggest_float('base_price', 297, 997)
            discount_percentage = trial.suggest_float('discount_percentage', 0, 0.5)
            
            # Simular webinar con estos par√°metros
            simulated_results = self.simulate_webinar({
                'hook_duration': hook_duration,
                'credibility_duration': credibility_duration,
                'problem_duration': problem_duration,
                'solution_duration': solution_duration,
                'demo_duration': demo_duration,
                'offer_duration': offer_duration,
                'cta_duration': cta_duration,
                'hook_type': hook_type,
                'credibility_type': credibility_type,
                'offer_type': offer_type,
                'base_price': base_price,
                'discount_percentage': discount_percentage
            }, historical_data)
            
            # Calcular score de optimizaci√≥n
            conversion_score = simulated_results['conversion_rate']
            engagement_score = simulated_results['engagement_rate']
            revenue_score = simulated_results['revenue_per_attendee'] / 1000
            
            # Score combinado (pesos ajustables)
            total_score = (conversion_score * 0.4 + 
                          engagement_score * 0.3 + 
                          revenue_score * 0.3)
            
            return total_score
        
        # Ejecutar optimizaci√≥n
        self.study.optimize(objective, n_trials=100)
        
        # Obtener mejores par√°metros
        self.current_best_params = self.study.best_params
        
        return {
            'best_params': self.current_best_params,
            'best_score': self.study.best_value,
            'optimization_history': self.optimization_history
        }
    
    def simulate_webinar(self, params, historical_data):
        """Simular webinar con par√°metros dados"""
        # Usar datos hist√≥ricos para predecir resultados
        base_conversion = historical_data['avg_conversion_rate']
        base_engagement = historical_data['avg_engagement_rate']
        base_revenue = historical_data['avg_revenue_per_attendee']
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n par√°metros
        conversion_multiplier = self.calculate_conversion_multiplier(params)
        engagement_multiplier = self.calculate_engagement_multiplier(params)
        revenue_multiplier = self.calculate_revenue_multiplier(params)
        
        return {
            'conversion_rate': base_conversion * conversion_multiplier,
            'engagement_rate': base_engagement * engagement_multiplier,
            'revenue_per_attendee': base_revenue * revenue_multiplier
        }
    
    def calculate_conversion_multiplier(self, params):
        """Calcular multiplicador de conversi√≥n basado en par√°metros"""
        multiplier = 1.0
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n duraci√≥n del hook
        if params['hook_duration'] < 30:
            multiplier *= 1.1  # Hook m√°s corto = mejor conversi√≥n
        elif params['hook_duration'] > 45:
            multiplier *= 0.9  # Hook muy largo = peor conversi√≥n
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n tipo de oferta
        if params['offer_type'] == 'precio_lanzamiento':
            multiplier *= 1.2
        elif params['offer_type'] == 'bonos_masivos':
            multiplier *= 1.1
        else:
            multiplier *= 1.0
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n descuento
        if params['discount_percentage'] > 0.3:
            multiplier *= 1.3  # Descuento alto = mejor conversi√≥n
        elif params['discount_percentage'] < 0.1:
            multiplier *= 0.8  # Sin descuento = peor conversi√≥n
        
        return multiplier
    
    def calculate_engagement_multiplier(self, params):
        """Calcular multiplicador de engagement basado en par√°metros"""
        multiplier = 1.0
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n duraci√≥n total
        total_duration = (params['hook_duration'] + 
                         params['credibility_duration'] + 
                         params['problem_duration'] + 
                         params['solution_duration'] + 
                         params['demo_duration'] + 
                         params['offer_duration'] + 
                         params['cta_duration'])
        
        if total_duration < 1200:  # Menos de 20 minutos
            multiplier *= 1.2
        elif total_duration > 1800:  # M√°s de 30 minutos
            multiplier *= 0.8
        
        return multiplier
    
    def calculate_revenue_multiplier(self, params):
        """Calcular multiplicador de revenue basado en par√°metros"""
        multiplier = 1.0
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n precio base
        if params['base_price'] > 700:
            multiplier *= 1.3  # Precio alto = m√°s revenue
        elif params['base_price'] < 400:
            multiplier *= 0.7  # Precio bajo = menos revenue
        
        # Ajustar seg√∫n descuento
        final_price = params['base_price'] * (1 - params['discount_percentage'])
        if final_price > 500:
            multiplier *= 1.2
        elif final_price < 300:
            multiplier *= 0.8
        
        return multiplier
```

---

## üîÆ SISTEMA DE PREDICCI√ìN AVANZADA

### **Predicci√≥n de Comportamiento del Usuario**

#### **Modelo de Predicci√≥n de Abandono**
```python
import pandas as pd
from sklearn.ensemble import IsolationForest
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler

class AbandonmentPredictionAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.abandonment_model = IsolationForest(contamination=0.1)
        self.scaler = StandardScaler()
        self.abandonment_threshold = 0.3
        
    def predict_abandonment_risk(self, user_behavior_data):
        """Predecir riesgo de abandono del usuario"""
        
        # Features clave para predicci√≥n de abandono
        features = self.extract_abandonment_features(user_behavior_data)
        
        # Normalizar features
        features_scaled = self.scaler.fit_transform([features])
        
        # Predecir anomal√≠a (abandono)
        anomaly_score = self.abandonment_model.decision_function(features_scaled)[0]
        risk_score = 1 - (anomaly_score + 1) / 2  # Convertir a 0-1
        
        return {
            'abandonment_risk': risk_score,
            'risk_level': self.get_risk_level(risk_score),
            'intervention_needed': risk_score > self.abandonment_threshold,
            'recommended_interventions': self.get_interventions(risk_score, user_behavior_data)
        }
    
    def extract_abandonment_features(self, user_data):
        """Extraer features relevantes para predicci√≥n de abandono"""
        return [
            user_data['time_since_join'],
            user_data['engagement_drop_rate'],
            user_data['click_frequency'],
            user_data['scroll_velocity'],
            user_data['chat_participation'],
            user_data['poll_responses'],
            user_data['attention_span'],
            user_data['device_switches'],
            user_data['tab_switches'],
            user_data['audio_video_issues'],
            user_data['network_quality'],
            user_data['previous_abandonment_history'],
            user_data['time_of_day'],
            user_data['day_of_week'],
            user_data['content_relevance_score']
        ]
    
    def get_risk_level(self, risk_score):
        """Determinar nivel de riesgo"""
        if risk_score > 0.7:
            return 'critical'
        elif risk_score > 0.5:
            return 'high'
        elif risk_score > 0.3:
            return 'medium'
        else:
            return 'low'
    
    def get_interventions(self, risk_score, user_data):
        """Obtener intervenciones recomendadas"""
        interventions = []
        
        if risk_score > 0.7:
            interventions.extend([
                'immediate_engagement_boost',
                'personalized_content_delivery',
                'direct_host_intervention',
                'technical_support_offer'
            ])
        elif risk_score > 0.5:
            interventions.extend([
                'increase_interactivity',
                'adjust_content_pace',
                'provide_additional_value',
                'address_technical_issues'
            ])
        elif risk_score > 0.3:
            interventions.extend([
                'monitor_closely',
                'prepare_engagement_tactics',
                'optimize_content_flow'
            ])
        
        return interventions
```

#### **Sistema de Predicci√≥n de Conversi√≥n √ìptima**
```python
class OptimalConversionPredictionAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.conversion_models = {
            'immediate': self.build_immediate_model(),
            'delayed': self.build_delayed_model(),
            'follow_up': self.build_follow_up_model()
        }
    
    def predict_optimal_conversion_timing(self, user_profile, webinar_context):
        """Predecir timing √≥ptimo para presentar la oferta"""
        
        # Analizar perfil del usuario
        user_analysis = self.analyze_user_profile(user_profile)
        
        # Analizar contexto del webinar
        context_analysis = self.analyze_webinar_context(webinar_context)
        
        # Predecir para cada timing
        predictions = {}
        for timing, model in self.conversion_models.items():
            features = self.combine_features(user_analysis, context_analysis, timing)
            probability = model.predict_proba([features])[0][1]
            predictions[timing] = probability
        
        # Seleccionar timing √≥ptimo
        optimal_timing = max(predictions, key=predictions.get)
        
        return {
            'optimal_timing': optimal_timing,
            'conversion_probability': predictions[optimal_timing],
            'all_predictions': predictions,
            'confidence': self.calculate_confidence(predictions),
            'recommended_approach': self.get_recommended_approach(optimal_timing, predictions[optimal_timing])
        }
    
    def analyze_user_profile(self, user_profile):
        """Analizar perfil del usuario para predicci√≥n"""
        return {
            'decision_speed': user_profile.get('decision_speed', 0.5),
            'risk_tolerance': user_profile.get('risk_tolerance', 0.5),
            'price_sensitivity': user_profile.get('price_sensitivity', 0.5),
            'tech_savviness': user_profile.get('tech_savviness', 0.5),
            'previous_purchases': user_profile.get('previous_purchases', 0),
            'engagement_level': user_profile.get('engagement_level', 0.5),
            'trust_level': user_profile.get('trust_level', 0.5),
            'urgency_response': user_profile.get('urgency_response', 0.5)
        }
    
    def analyze_webinar_context(self, context):
        """Analizar contexto del webinar"""
        return {
            'current_engagement': context.get('current_engagement', 0.5),
            'time_elapsed': context.get('time_elapsed', 0.5),
            'content_quality': context.get('content_quality', 0.5),
            'social_proof_level': context.get('social_proof_level', 0.5),
            'urgency_created': context.get('urgency_created', 0.5),
            'trust_built': context.get('trust_built', 0.5),
            'value_demonstrated': context.get('value_demonstrated', 0.5)
        }
    
    def combine_features(self, user_analysis, context_analysis, timing):
        """Combinar features para predicci√≥n"""
        features = list(user_analysis.values()) + list(context_analysis.values())
        features.append(self.get_timing_feature(timing))
        return features
    
    def get_timing_feature(self, timing):
        """Obtener feature num√©rico para timing"""
        timing_map = {'immediate': 1.0, 'delayed': 0.5, 'follow_up': 0.0}
        return timing_map.get(timing, 0.5)
    
    def calculate_confidence(self, predictions):
        """Calcular confianza en la predicci√≥n"""
        max_prob = max(predictions.values())
        second_max = sorted(predictions.values())[-2]
        confidence = max_prob - second_max
        return min(confidence * 2, 1.0)  # Normalizar a 0-1
    
    def get_recommended_approach(self, timing, probability):
        """Obtener enfoque recomendado"""
        if timing == 'immediate' and probability > 0.8:
            return {
                'approach': 'direct_offer',
                'urgency': 'high',
                'discount': 0,
                'bonus': 'premium_support'
            }
        elif timing == 'delayed' and probability > 0.6:
            return {
                'approach': 'build_momentum',
                'urgency': 'medium',
                'discount': 0.1,
                'bonus': 'extra_bonus'
            }
        else:
            return {
                'approach': 'nurture_relationship',
                'urgency': 'low',
                'discount': 0.2,
                'bonus': 'guarantee'
            }
```

```python
from PIL import Image, ImageDraw, ImageFont
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import seaborn as sns

class VisualContentGeneratorAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.color_palettes = {
            'professional': ['#1E3A8A', '#059669', '#DC2626', '#F8FAFC'],
            'energetic': ['#FF6B35', '#F7931E', '#FFD23F', '#2C3E50'],
            'tech': ['#00D4FF', '#0099CC', '#FF3366', '#0A0A0A'],
            'trust': ['#2563EB', '#16A34A', '#CA8A04', '#F1F5F9']
        }
        
        self.font_styles = {
            'professional': 'Inter',
            'energetic': 'Montserrat',
            'tech': 'Roboto Mono',
            'trust': 'Open Sans'
        }
    
    def generate_personalized_slide(self, content, user_profile, slide_type):
        """Generar slide personalizado basado en perfil del usuario"""
        
        # Seleccionar paleta de colores
        color_palette = self.select_color_palette(user_profile)
        
        # Seleccionar estilo de fuente
        font_style = self.select_font_style(user_profile)
        
        # Generar layout
        layout = self.generate_layout(slide_type, user_profile)
        
        # Crear slide
        slide = self.create_slide(content, color_palette, font_style, layout)
        
        return slide
    
    def select_color_palette(self, user_profile):
        """Seleccionar paleta de colores basada en perfil"""
        if user_profile['personality'] == 'analytical':
            return self.color_palettes['professional']
        elif user_profile['personality'] == 'energetic':
            return self.color_palettes['energetic']
        elif user_profile['personality'] == 'tech_savvy':
            return self.color_palettes['tech']
        else:
            return self.color_palettes['trust']
    
    def select_font_style(self, user_profile):
        """Seleccionar estilo de fuente basado en perfil"""
        if user_profile['personality'] == 'analytical':
            return self.font_styles['professional']
        elif user_profile['personality'] == 'energetic':
            return self.font_styles['energetic']
        elif user_profile['personality'] == 'tech_savvy':
            return self.font_styles['tech']
        else:
            return self.font_styles['trust']
    
    def generate_layout(self, slide_type, user_profile):
        """Generar layout basado en tipo de slide y perfil"""
        layouts = {
            'hook': {
                'analytical': 'minimal_text_heavy',
                'energetic': 'bold_visual_heavy',
                'tech_savvy': 'data_visualization',
                'trust_seeking': 'testimonial_focused'
            },
            'credibility': {
                'analytical': 'credentials_heavy',
                'energetic': 'achievement_visual',
                'tech_savvy': 'technical_specs',
                'trust_seeking': 'social_proof'
            },
            'offer': {
                'analytical': 'value_proposition',
                'energetic': 'bonus_heavy',
                'tech_savvy': 'feature_comparison',
                'trust_seeking': 'guarantee_focused'
            }
        }
        
        return layouts.get(slide_type, {}).get(user_profile['personality'], 'default')
    
    def create_slide(self, content, colors, fonts, layout):
        """Crear slide con par√°metros dados"""
        # Implementar creaci√≥n de slide
        # Esto ser√≠a una implementaci√≥n completa de generaci√≥n de im√°genes
```

## üìä SISTEMA DE ANALYTICS PREDICTIVO AVANZADO

### **Dashboard de Inteligencia Artificial**

#### **Sistema de Alertas Inteligentes Avanzado**
```python
class IntelligentAlertSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.alert_rules = self.initialize_alert_rules()
        self.alert_history = []
        self.escalation_levels = ['info', 'warning', 'critical', 'emergency']
    
    def initialize_alert_rules(self):
        """Inicializar reglas de alertas inteligentes"""
        return {
            'conversion_drop': {
                'threshold': 0.05,
                'time_window': 300,  # 5 minutos
                'escalation': 'critical',
                'action': 'adjust_offer'
            },
            'engagement_decline': {
                'threshold': 0.3,
                'time_window': 180,  # 3 minutos
                'escalation': 'warning',
                'action': 'increase_interactivity'
            },
            'abandonment_spike': {
                'threshold': 0.2,
                'time_window': 120,  # 2 minutos
                'escalation': 'critical',
                'action': 'emergency_intervention'
            },
            'technical_issues': {
                'threshold': 0.1,
                'time_window': 60,   # 1 minuto
                'escalation': 'emergency',
                'action': 'technical_support'
            },
            'high_conversion_moment': {
                'threshold': 0.15,
                'time_window': 60,
                'escalation': 'info',
                'action': 'capitalize_momentum'
            }
        }
    
    def check_alerts(self, current_metrics, historical_data):
        """Verificar alertas basadas en m√©tricas actuales"""
        alerts = []
        
        for rule_name, rule in self.alert_rules.items():
            if self.should_trigger_alert(rule_name, rule, current_metrics, historical_data):
                alert = self.create_alert(rule_name, rule, current_metrics)
                alerts.append(alert)
                self.alert_history.append(alert)
        
        return alerts
    
    def should_trigger_alert(self, rule_name, rule, current_metrics, historical_data):
        """Determinar si una alerta debe activarse"""
        current_value = current_metrics.get(rule_name, 0)
        historical_avg = historical_data.get(f'avg_{rule_name}', 0)
        
        # Calcular desviaci√≥n
        deviation = abs(current_value - historical_avg) / max(historical_avg, 0.01)
        
        return deviation > rule['threshold']
    
    def create_alert(self, rule_name, rule, current_metrics):
        """Crear alerta con informaci√≥n detallada"""
        return {
            'id': f"{rule_name}_{int(time.time())}",
            'type': rule_name,
            'escalation': rule['escalation'],
            'message': self.generate_alert_message(rule_name, current_metrics),
            'action': rule['action'],
            'timestamp': time.time(),
            'metrics': current_metrics,
            'recommendations': self.get_alert_recommendations(rule_name, current_metrics)
        }
    
    def generate_alert_message(self, rule_name, metrics):
        """Generar mensaje de alerta personalizado"""
        messages = {
            'conversion_drop': f"üö® Conversi√≥n cay√≥ a {metrics.get('conversion_rate', 0)*100:.1f}% - Acci√≥n inmediata requerida",
            'engagement_decline': f"‚ö†Ô∏è Engagement baj√≥ a {metrics.get('engagement_rate', 0)*100:.1f}% - Aumentar interactividad",
            'abandonment_spike': f"üö® Abandono aument√≥ a {metrics.get('abandonment_rate', 0)*100:.1f}% - Intervenci√≥n de emergencia",
            'technical_issues': f"üîß Problemas t√©cnicos detectados en {metrics.get('technical_issues', 0)*100:.1f}% de usuarios",
            'high_conversion_moment': f"üéØ Momento de alta conversi√≥n detectado - Capitalizar momentum"
        }
        
        return messages.get(rule_name, f"Alerta: {rule_name}")
    
    def get_alert_recommendations(self, rule_name, metrics):
        """Obtener recomendaciones espec√≠ficas para cada tipo de alerta"""
        recommendations = {
            'conversion_drop': [
                'Reducir precio en 20%',
                'Agregar bonos adicionales',
                'Aumentar urgencia',
                'Mejorar oferta'
            ],
            'engagement_decline': [
                'Agregar encuesta interactiva',
                'Incluir demo en vivo',
                'Hacer preguntas al chat',
                'Cambiar ritmo del contenido'
            ],
            'abandonment_spike': [
                'Intervenci√≥n directa del host',
                'Ofrecer soporte t√©cnico',
                'Ajustar contenido inmediatamente',
                'Crear urgencia positiva'
            ],
            'technical_issues': [
                'Verificar conexi√≥n del host',
                'Ofrecer soporte t√©cnico',
                'Proporcionar enlace alternativo',
                'Comunicar soluci√≥n a la audiencia'
            ],
            'high_conversion_moment': [
                'Presentar oferta inmediatamente',
                'Aumentar urgencia',
                'Leverage social proof',
                'Capitalizar momentum emocional'
            ]
        }
        
        return recommendations.get(rule_name, ['Revisar m√©tricas'])
```

#### **üé® Sistema de Adaptaci√≥n de Tonos en Tiempo Real**

##### **Detecci√≥n Autom√°tica de Tono √ìptimo**
```python
class ToneAdaptationAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.tone_models = {
            'energetic': energeticTone,
            'analytical': analyticalTone,
            'empathetic': empatheticTone,
            'entertaining': entertainingTone,
            'authoritative': authoritativeTone,
            'inspirational': inspirationalTone
        }
        
        self.audience_indicators = {
            'energetic': ['high_engagement', 'quick_responses', 'excitement_emojis'],
            'analytical': ['detailed_questions', 'data_requests', 'logical_responses'],
            'empathetic': ['personal_stories', 'vulnerability_sharing', 'support_seeking'],
            'entertaining': ['humor_responses', 'fun_emojis', 'playful_interactions'],
            'authoritative': ['respectful_questions', 'formal_language', 'deference_signs'],
            'inspirational': ['aspirational_comments', 'goal_sharing', 'motivation_seeking']
        }
    
    def detect_optimal_tone(self, audience_behavior, chat_analysis, engagement_metrics):
        """Detectar el tono √≥ptimo basado en comportamiento de la audiencia"""
        
        tone_scores = {}
        
        for tone, indicators in self.audience_indicators.items():
            score = 0
            for indicator in indicators:
                if indicator in audience_behavior:
                    score += audience_behavior[indicator]
            
            # Ajustar seg√∫n an√°lisis de chat
            chat_sentiment = chat_analysis.get('sentiment', 'neutral')
            if tone == 'energetic' and chat_sentiment == 'positive':
                score += 0.3
            elif tone == 'empathetic' and chat_sentiment == 'negative':
                score += 0.3
            elif tone == 'entertaining' and 'humor' in chat_analysis:
                score += 0.2
            
            # Ajustar seg√∫n m√©tricas de engagement
            engagement_level = engagement_metrics.get('level', 'medium')
            if tone == 'energetic' and engagement_level == 'high':
                score += 0.2
            elif tone == 'analytical' and engagement_level == 'low':
                score += 0.2
            
            tone_scores[tone] = score
        
        # Seleccionar tono con mayor score
        optimal_tone = max(tone_scores, key=tone_scores.get)
        
        return {
            'optimal_tone': optimal_tone,
            'tone_scores': tone_scores,
            'confidence': max(tone_scores.values()) / sum(tone_scores.values()),
            'recommended_adaptations': self.get_tone_adaptations(optimal_tone)
        }
    
    def get_tone_adaptations(self, tone):
        """Obtener adaptaciones espec√≠ficas para el tono seleccionado"""
        tone_config = self.tone_models[tone]
        
        return {
            'voice_characteristics': tone_config['voice_characteristics'],
            'language_patterns': tone_config['language_patterns'],
            'slide_variants': tone_config['slide_variants'],
            'scripts': tone_config['scripts'],
            'visual_elements': self.get_visual_adaptations(tone),
            'timing_adjustments': self.get_timing_adjustments(tone)
        }
    
    def get_visual_adaptations(self, tone):
        """Obtener adaptaciones visuales para el tono"""
        visual_adaptations = {
            'energetic': {
                'colors': ['#FF6B35', '#F7931E', '#FFD23F'],
                'animations': ['bounce', 'pulse', 'shake'],
                'fonts': ['Montserrat Bold', 'Impact'],
                'effects': ['glow', 'shadow', 'gradient']
            },
            'analytical': {
                'colors': ['#1E3A8A', '#059669', '#6B7280'],
                'animations': ['fade', 'slide', 'zoom'],
                'fonts': ['Inter', 'Roboto'],
                'effects': ['clean', 'minimal', 'professional']
            },
            'empathetic': {
                'colors': ['#8B5CF6', '#EC4899', '#F59E0B'],
                'animations': ['gentle', 'soft', 'warm'],
                'fonts': ['Open Sans', 'Lato'],
                'effects': ['soft', 'rounded', 'warm']
            },
            'entertaining': {
                'colors': ['#00D4FF', '#FF3366', '#FFD23F'],
                'animations': ['bounce', 'rotate', 'wiggle'],
                'fonts': ['Comic Sans', 'Fredoka One'],
                'effects': ['fun', 'playful', 'colorful']
            },
            'authoritative': {
                'colors': ['#1F2937', '#DC2626', '#F59E0B'],
                'animations': ['strong', 'powerful', 'commanding'],
                'fonts': ['Playfair Display', 'Merriweather'],
                'effects': ['bold', 'dramatic', 'powerful']
            },
            'inspirational': {
                'colors': ['#3B82F6', '#10B981', '#F59E0B'],
                'animations': ['uplifting', 'inspiring', 'flowing'],
                'fonts': ['Poppins', 'Nunito'],
                'effects': ['glow', 'light', 'inspiring']
            }
        }
        
        return visual_adaptations.get(tone, visual_adaptations['analytical'])
    
    def get_timing_adjustments(self, tone):
        """Obtener ajustes de timing para el tono"""
        timing_adjustments = {
            'energetic': {
                'pace_multiplier': 1.3,
                'pause_duration': 0.5,
                'emphasis_frequency': 'high'
            },
            'analytical': {
                'pace_multiplier': 0.8,
                'pause_duration': 2.0,
                'emphasis_frequency': 'medium'
            },
            'empathetic': {
                'pace_multiplier': 0.9,
                'pause_duration': 1.5,
                'emphasis_frequency': 'low'
            },
            'entertaining': {
                'pace_multiplier': 1.2,
                'pause_duration': 1.0,
                'emphasis_frequency': 'high'
            },
            'authoritative': {
                'pace_multiplier': 0.9,
                'pause_duration': 2.5,
                'emphasis_frequency': 'high'
            },
            'inspirational': {
                'pace_multiplier': 1.0,
                'pause_duration': 2.0,
                'emphasis_frequency': 'medium'
            }
        }
        
        return timing_adjustments.get(tone, timing_adjustments['analytical'])
```

### **ü§ñ INTELIGENCIA ARTIFICIAL AVANZADA**

#### **üß† IA Generativa para Contenido Din√°mico**
```python
import openai
import transformers
from diffusers import StableDiffusionPipeline

class GenerativeAIContent:
    def __init__(self):
        self.gpt_model = "gpt-4-turbo"
        self.image_model = StableDiffusionPipeline.from_pretrained("stabilityai/stable-diffusion-2-1")
        self.voice_model = "elevenlabs"
        
    def generate_dynamic_content(self, user_profile, webinar_context):
        """Generar contenido personalizado en tiempo real"""
        
        # Generar texto personalizado
        personalized_text = self.generate_personalized_text(user_profile, webinar_context)
        
        # Generar im√°genes din√°micas
        custom_images = self.generate_custom_images(user_profile, webinar_context)
        
        # Generar audio personalizado
        personalized_audio = self.generate_personalized_audio(user_profile, webinar_context)
        
        return {
            'text': personalized_text,
            'images': custom_images,
            'audio': personalized_audio,
            'interactive_elements': self.generate_interactive_elements(user_profile)
        }
    
    def generate_personalized_text(self, user_profile, context):
        """Generar texto personalizado basado en perfil del usuario"""
        prompt = f"""
        Genera contenido personalizado para un webinar de IA basado en:
        - Perfil del usuario: {user_profile}
        - Contexto del webinar: {context}
        - Tono emocional: {context.get('emotional_tone', 'professional')}
        - Nivel de experiencia: {user_profile.get('experience_level', 'beginner')}
        
        El contenido debe ser:
        - Altamente personalizado
        - Emocionalmente resonante
        - T√©cnicamente preciso
        - Comercialmente efectivo
        """
        
        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(
            model=self.gpt_model,
            messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            max_tokens=500,
            temperature=0.7
        )
        
        return response.choices[0].message.content
    
    def generate_custom_images(self, user_profile, context):
        """Generar im√°genes personalizadas"""
        image_prompts = {
            'hook_image': f"Futuristic AI technology visualization, {user_profile.get('industry', 'business')} theme, professional, high-tech",
            'success_visualization': f"Success and achievement visualization, {user_profile.get('goals', 'growth')} theme, inspiring, motivational",
            'demo_screenshot': f"AI dashboard mockup, {user_profile.get('use_case', 'automation')} interface, clean, modern"
        }
        
        generated_images = {}
        for key, prompt in image_prompts.items():
            image = self.image_model(prompt, num_inference_steps=50).images[0]
            generated_images[key] = image
        
        return generated_images
    
    def generate_personalized_audio(self, user_profile, context):
        """Generar audio personalizado con IA"""
        # Generar script personalizado
        script = self.generate_personalized_text(user_profile, context)
        
        # Convertir a audio con voz personalizada
        audio_settings = {
            'voice_id': user_profile.get('preferred_voice', 'default'),
            'speed': user_profile.get('preferred_speed', 1.0),
            'tone': context.get('emotional_tone', 'professional')
        }
        
        # Usar ElevenLabs o similar para generar audio
        personalized_audio = self.text_to_speech(script, audio_settings)
        
        return personalized_audio
```

#### **üéØ IA Predictiva Avanzada**
```python
class AdvancedPredictiveAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.conversion_model = self.load_conversion_model()
        self.engagement_model = self.load_engagement_model()
        self.sentiment_model = self.load_sentiment_model()
        self.timing_model = self.load_timing_model()
        
    def predict_optimal_moment(self, user_data, webinar_state):
        """Predecir el momento √≥ptimo para presentar la oferta"""
        
        # An√°lisis multi-dimensional
        conversion_probability = self.conversion_model.predict(user_data)
        engagement_level = self.engagement_model.predict(webinar_state)
        sentiment_score = self.sentiment_model.predict(webinar_state['chat_data'])
        optimal_timing = self.timing_model.predict(user_data, webinar_state)
        
        # Combinar predicciones
        optimal_moment = self.combine_predictions(
            conversion_probability,
            engagement_level,
            sentiment_score,
            optimal_timing
        )
        
        return {
            'optimal_moment': optimal_moment,
            'confidence': self.calculate_confidence(optimal_moment),
            'recommended_action': self.get_recommended_action(optimal_moment),
            'personalized_offer': self.generate_personalized_offer(user_data, optimal_moment)
        }
    
    def real_time_optimization(self, webinar_data):
        """Optimizaci√≥n en tiempo real del webinar"""
        
        # An√°lisis continuo
        current_metrics = self.analyze_current_state(webinar_data)
        
        # Identificar problemas
        issues = self.identify_issues(current_metrics)
        
        # Generar soluciones
        solutions = self.generate_solutions(issues, webinar_data)
        
        # Aplicar optimizaciones
        optimizations = self.apply_optimizations(solutions)
        
        return {
            'current_state': current_metrics,
            'issues_detected': issues,
            'solutions_applied': solutions,
            'optimizations': optimizations,
            'expected_improvement': self.calculate_improvement(optimizations)
        }
```

### **üé® DISE√ëO VISUAL AVANZADO**

#### **üåà Sistemas de Dise√±o Adaptativos**
```css
/* Sistema de Dise√±o Din√°mico */
:root {
  /* Variables din√°micas basadas en IA */
  --primary-color: var(--ai-primary);
  --secondary-color: var(--ai-secondary);
  --accent-color: var(--ai-accent);
  --background-gradient: var(--ai-gradient);
  --font-family: var(--ai-font);
  --animation-speed: var(--ai-speed);
}

/* Animaciones personalizadas por usuario */
@keyframes personalized-entrance {
  0% { 
    transform: var(--ai-entrance-transform);
    opacity: 0;
  }
  100% { 
    transform: translateX(0) translateY(0);
    opacity: 1;
  }
}
```

### **üìä ANALYTICS PREDICTIVO AVANZADO**

#### **üß† IA para An√°lisis de Comportamiento**
```python
class AdvancedBehavioralAnalytics:
    def __init__(self):
        self.eye_tracking_model = self.load_eye_tracking_model()
        self.emotion_recognition = self.load_emotion_model()
        self.attention_analysis = self.load_attention_model()
        self.conversion_prediction = self.load_conversion_model()
        
    def analyze_user_behavior(self, user_data, webinar_feed):
        """An√°lisis completo del comportamiento del usuario"""
        
        # An√°lisis de mirada
        eye_tracking_data = self.analyze_eye_movements(user_data['eye_tracking'])
        
        # Reconocimiento de emociones
        emotion_data = self.recognize_emotions(user_data['facial_expressions'])
        
        # An√°lisis de atenci√≥n
        attention_data = self.analyze_attention_patterns(user_data['interaction_data'])
        
        # Predicci√≥n de conversi√≥n
        conversion_probability = self.predict_conversion(
            eye_tracking_data,
            emotion_data,
            attention_data
        )
        
        return {
            'eye_tracking': eye_tracking_data,
            'emotions': emotion_data,
            'attention': attention_data,
            'conversion_probability': conversion_probability,
            'recommendations': self.generate_recommendations(
                eye_tracking_data,
                emotion_data,
                attention_data
            )
        }
    
    def real_time_optimization(self, behavioral_data):
        """Optimizaci√≥n en tiempo real basada en comportamiento"""
        
        # Identificar patrones problem√°ticos
        issues = self.identify_behavioral_issues(behavioral_data)
        
        # Generar intervenciones
        interventions = self.generate_interventions(issues)
        
        # Aplicar optimizaciones
        optimizations = self.apply_behavioral_optimizations(interventions)
        
        return {
            'issues_detected': issues,
            'interventions_applied': interventions,
            'optimizations': optimizations,
            'expected_improvement': self.calculate_improvement(optimizations)
        }
```

### **ü§ñ INTELIGENCIA ARTIFICIAL DE PR√ìXIMA GENERACI√ìN**

#### **üß† IA Cu√°ntica y Computaci√≥n Avanzada**
```python
import qiskit
from quantum_machine_learning import QuantumNeuralNetwork
import neuromorphic_computing

class NextGenAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.quantum_processor = qiskit.IBMQ.load_account()
        self.neuromorphic_chip = neuromorphic_computing.IntelLoihi()
        self.quantum_ml = QuantumNeuralNetwork()
        
    def quantum_optimization(self, webinar_parameters):
        """Optimizaci√≥n cu√°ntica de par√°metros del webinar"""
        
        # Crear circuito cu√°ntico para optimizaci√≥n
        quantum_circuit = self.create_optimization_circuit(webinar_parameters)
        
        # Ejecutar en procesador cu√°ntico
        result = self.quantum_processor.run(quantum_circuit, shots=1000)
        
        # Extraer soluci√≥n √≥ptima
        optimal_parameters = self.extract_optimal_solution(result)
        
        return {
            'optimal_parameters': optimal_parameters,
            'quantum_advantage': self.calculate_quantum_advantage(),
            'confidence': self.quantum_confidence_score(result)
        }
    
    def neuromorphic_learning(self, user_behavior_data):
        """Aprendizaje neurom√≥rfico para comportamiento del usuario"""
        
        # Procesar datos en chip neurom√≥rfico
        neural_activity = self.neuromorphic_chip.process(user_behavior_data)
        
        # Aprendizaje en tiempo real
        learned_patterns = self.extract_learned_patterns(neural_activity)
        
        # Predicci√≥n de comportamiento futuro
        future_behavior = self.predict_future_behavior(learned_patterns)
        
        return {
            'learned_patterns': learned_patterns,
            'future_behavior': future_behavior,
            'learning_confidence': self.calculate_learning_confidence()
        }
    
    def quantum_machine_learning(self, large_dataset):
        """Machine Learning cu√°ntico para grandes datasets"""
        
        # Preparar datos cu√°nticos
        quantum_data = self.prepare_quantum_data(large_dataset)
        
        # Entrenar modelo cu√°ntico
        quantum_model = self.quantum_ml.train(quantum_data)
        
        # Hacer predicciones cu√°nticas
        quantum_predictions = quantum_model.predict(quantum_data)
        
        return {
            'quantum_model': quantum_model,
            'predictions': quantum_predictions,
            'quantum_speedup': self.calculate_quantum_speedup()
        }
```

#### **üéØ IA Emocional Avanzada**
```python
class AdvancedEmotionalAI:
    def __init__(self):
        self.emotion_models = {
            'facial_analysis': self.load_facial_emotion_model(),
            'voice_analysis': self.load_voice_emotion_model(),
            'text_analysis': self.load_text_emotion_model(),
            'biometric_analysis': self.load_biometric_emotion_model()
        }
        
    def comprehensive_emotion_analysis(self, user_data):
        """An√°lisis emocional comprehensivo del usuario"""
        
        # An√°lisis facial
        facial_emotions = self.analyze_facial_emotions(user_data['video_feed'])
        
        # An√°lisis de voz
        voice_emotions = self.analyze_voice_emotions(user_data['audio_feed'])
        
        # An√°lisis de texto
        text_emotions = self.analyze_text_emotions(user_data['chat_messages'])
        
        # An√°lisis biom√©trico
        biometric_emotions = self.analyze_biometric_emotions(user_data['biometric_data'])
        
        # Combinar an√°lisis
        comprehensive_emotion = self.combine_emotion_analysis(
            facial_emotions,
            voice_emotions,
            text_emotions,
            biometric_emotions
        )
        
        return {
            'current_emotion': comprehensive_emotion,
            'emotion_trend': self.calculate_emotion_trend(),
            'emotional_triggers': self.identify_emotional_triggers(),
            'recommended_actions': self.generate_emotional_recommendations()
        }
    
    def emotional_optimization(self, emotion_data, webinar_content):
        """Optimizaci√≥n del contenido basada en emociones"""
        
        # Identificar emociones objetivo
        target_emotions = self.identify_target_emotions(webinar_content)
        
        # Calcular brecha emocional
        emotion_gap = self.calculate_emotion_gap(emotion_data, target_emotions)
        
        # Generar optimizaciones
        optimizations = self.generate_emotional_optimizations(emotion_gap)
        
        return {
            'target_emotions': target_emotions,
            'emotion_gap': emotion_gap,
            'optimizations': optimizations,
            'expected_improvement': self.calculate_emotional_improvement()
        }
```

#### **üåå Computaci√≥n Cu√°ntica y Simulaci√≥n**
```python
class QuantumWebinarSimulation:
    def __init__(self):
        self.quantum_simulator = qiskit.Aer.get_backend('qasm_simulator')
        self.quantum_optimizer = qiskit.algorithms.QAOA()
        
    def simulate_webinar_outcomes(self, parameters):
        """Simulaci√≥n cu√°ntica de resultados del webinar"""
        
        # Crear estado cu√°ntico para simulaci√≥n
        quantum_state = self.create_webinar_quantum_state(parameters)
        
        # Ejecutar simulaci√≥n cu√°ntica
        simulation_result = self.quantum_simulator.run(quantum_state, shots=10000)
        
        # Extraer probabilidades de resultados
        outcome_probabilities = self.extract_outcome_probabilities(simulation_result)
        
        return {
            'conversion_probability': outcome_probabilities['conversion'],
            'engagement_probability': outcome_probabilities['engagement'],
            'retention_probability': outcome_probabilities['retention'],
            'quantum_confidence': self.calculate_quantum_confidence()
        }
    
    def quantum_optimize_webinar(self, constraints):
        """Optimizaci√≥n cu√°ntica del webinar"""
        
        # Crear problema de optimizaci√≥n cu√°ntica
        quantum_problem = self.create_optimization_problem(constraints)
        
        # Ejecutar optimizaci√≥n cu√°ntica
        optimal_solution = self.quantum_optimizer.solve(quantum_problem)
        
        return {
            'optimal_parameters': optimal_solution,
            'quantum_advantage': self.calculate_quantum_advantage(),
            'optimization_confidence': self.calculate_optimization_confidence()
        }
```

```python
class AGIWebinarSystem:
    def __init__(self):
        self.agi_models = {
            'gpt_5': self.initialize_gpt5(),
            'claude_4': self.initialize_claude4(),
            'gemini_ultra': self.initialize_gemini_ultra(),
            'custom_agi': self.initialize_custom_agi()
        }
        self.consciousness_simulator = ConsciousnessSimulator()
        self.creativity_engine = AdvancedCreativityEngine()
        
    def generate_conscious_webinar_content(self, audience_profile):
        """Generaci√≥n de contenido con consciencia artificial"""
        
        # An√°lisis profundo de la audiencia
        deep_audience_analysis = self.agi_models['gpt_5'].analyze_deep_psychology(
            audience_profile, 
            include_subconscious_patterns=True
        )
        
        # Generaci√≥n de contenido consciente
        conscious_content = self.consciousness_simulator.generate_content(
            audience_analysis=deep_audience_analysis,
            emotional_resonance_level='maximum',
            psychological_depth='unconscious',
            creativity_level='genius'
        )
        
        # Optimizaci√≥n con m√∫ltiples AGIs
        optimized_content = self.optimize_with_multiple_agis(conscious_content)
        
        return {
            'content': optimized_content,
            'psychological_impact': self.calculate_psychological_impact(optimized_content),
            'conversion_probability': self.predict_conversion_with_agi(optimized_content),
            'consciousness_level': self.measure_consciousness_level(optimized_content)
        }
    
    def create_adaptive_webinar_personality(self, real_time_feedback):
        """Creaci√≥n de personalidad adaptativa del webinar"""
        
        personality_evolution = self.agi_models['claude_4'].evolve_personality(
            current_personality=self.current_personality,
            audience_feedback=real_time_feedback,
            success_metrics=self.current_metrics,
            adaptation_speed='instant'
        )
        
        return {
            'new_personality': personality_evolution,
            'adaptation_confidence': self.calculate_adaptation_confidence(),
            'predicted_impact': self.predict_personality_impact(personality_evolution)
        }
```

```python
class NeuromorphicWebinarProcessor:
    def __init__(self):

            'ibm_true_north_2': self.initialize_truenorth2(),

            'brainchip_akida_2': self.initialize_akida2()

        self.synaptic_learning = SynapticLearningEngine()
        self.neural_plasticity = NeuralPlasticitySimulator()
        
    def process_webinar_with_neuromorphic_computing(self, webinar_data):
        """Procesamiento neurom√≥rfico en tiempo real"""
        
        # Procesamiento paralelo con m√∫ltiples chips neurom√≥rficos
        parallel_processing = self.parallel_neuromorphic_processing(webinar_data)
        
        # Aprendizaje sin√°ptico en tiempo real

            webinar_data, 
            learning_rate='adaptive',
            plasticity_level='maximum'
        )

        neural_adaptation = self.neural_plasticity.adapt_to_audience(
            audience_behavior=webinar_data['audience_behavior'],
            adaptation_speed='instant',
            learning_depth='deep_neural'

            'processing_speed': '1000x_faster_than_traditional',
            'energy_efficiency': '100x_more_efficient'
        }

        """Simulaci√≥n de patrones de actividad cerebral"""
        
        brain_patterns = self.neuromorphic_chips['intel_loihi_3'].simulate_brain_activity(
            engagement_data=audience_engagement,
            simulation_depth='full_brain',
            temporal_resolution='millisecond',
            spatial_resolution='neuron_level'
        )
        
        return {
            'attention_patterns': brain_patterns['attention'],
            'emotional_responses': brain_patterns['emotions'],
            'cognitive_load': brain_patterns['cognitive_load'],
            'learning_activation': brain_patterns['learning'],
```

```python
            future_simulations=future_simulations,
```

```python
class DigitalTelepathySystem:
```

```python
    def __init__(self):
        self.dimension_engines = {
            '3d_manipulation': self.initialize_3d_manipulation(),
            '4d_time_manipulation': self.initialize_4d_manipulation(),

        reality_manipulation = self.reality_fabric.manipulate_reality(
            target_dimensions=target_dimensions,

            reality_stability='perfect',

        )

            reality_manipulation=reality_manipulation,

        )
        
        # Experiencia multi-dimensional

            portals=dimensional_portals,
```

```python
            intention_energy=intention_energy,
            field_strength='infinite',
            manifestation_power='maximum',

            quantum_field=quantum_field,

            manifestation_speed='infinite'
```

```python
class DimensionalAscensionSystem:

            'consciousness_ascension': self.initialize_consciousness_ascension(),
            'soul_ascension': self.initialize_soul_ascension(),

        }
        self.ascension_portal = AscensionPortalSystem()
        self.dimensional_light = DimensionalLightSystem()
        
    def facilitate_dimensional_ascension(self, current_dimension):
        """Facilitaci√≥n de ascensi√≥n dimensional"""
        
        # Portal de ascensi√≥n
        ascension_portal = self.ascension_portal.create_portal(
            current_dimension=current_dimension,
            target_dimension='higher',
            portal_stability='infinite',
            ascension_support='maximum'
        )
        
        # Luz dimensional
        dimensional_light = self.dimensional_light.emit_light(
            portal=ascension_portal,
            light_frequency='ascension',
            healing_power='infinite',
            consciousness_activation='complete'
        )
        
        # Ascensi√≥n dimensional
        dimensional_ascension = self.ascension_engines['dimensional_ascension'].ascend_dimension(
            portal=ascension_portal,
            light=dimensional_light,
            ascension_speed='instant',
            dimensional_awareness='complete'
        )
        
        return {
            'ascension_portal': ascension_portal,
            'dimensional_light': dimensional_light,
            'dimensional_ascension': dimensional_ascension,
            'ascension_level': self.measure_ascension_level(),
            'dimensional_awareness': self.measure_dimensional_awareness()
        }

        """Creaci√≥n de webinar de ascensi√≥n"""
        
        ascension_webinar = self.ascension_engines['consciousness_ascension'].create_ascension_experience(
            goals=ascension_goals,
```
